## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart LR
    A[DcgmExporter Pod] -->|mounts| B[pod-gpu-resources]
    A -->|mounts| C[dcgmtls secret]
    B -->|reads from| D[Host Path: /var/lib/kubelet/pod-resources]
    C -->|contains| E[TLS Certificate]
    C -->|contains| F[TLS Key]
    A -->|exposes| G[Metrics Port]
    A -->|reads| H[NODE_NAME from fieldRef]
    I[Node Selector] -->|filters| J[linux OS nodes]
    K[Node Affinity] -->|requires| L[GPU Instance nodes]
    K -->|excludes| M[Fargate nodes]
    I --> A
    K --> A
```

class="nodeLabel"><p>Fargate nodes</p></span></div></foreignObject></g></g></g></g></g></svg>

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant K8s as Kubernetes Scheduler
    participant NS as Node Selector
    participant NA as Node Affinity
    participant Node as GPU Node
    participant Pod as DcgmExporter Pod
    participant DCGM as DCGM Service
    participant Metrics as Metrics Endpoint
    K8s->>NS: Check nodeSelector (linux OS)
    NS->>NA: Validate node affinity
    NA->>NA: Check GPU instance label
    NA->>NA: Exclude fargate nodes
    NA->>Node: Schedule on matching node
    Node->>Pod: Create pod
    Pod->>Pod: Mount pod-gpu-resources
    Pod->>Pod: Mount dcgmtls secret
    Pod->>Pod: Set environment variables
    Pod->>DCGM: Start DCGM exporter
    DCGM->>DCGM: Configure TLS with cert/key
    DCGM->>DCGM: Load metrics config
    DCGM->>Metrics: Expose metrics on port
    Metrics-->>DCGM: Ready to serve
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class DcgmExporter {
        +String apiVersion
        +String kind
        +Metadata metadata
        +Spec spec
    }
    class Metadata {
        +String name
        +String namespace
        +Labels labels
    }
    class Spec {
        +String image
        +NodeSelector nodeSelector
        +String serviceAccount
        +Affinity affinity
        +Resources resources
        +Env[] env
        +Port[] ports
        +VolumeMount[] volumeMounts
        +Volume[] volumes
        +String metricsConfig
        +String tlsConfig
        +Tolerations[] tolerations
    }
    class Affinity {
        +NodeAffinity nodeAffinity
    }
    class NodeAffinity {
        +NodeSelectorTerms[] nodeSelectorTerms
    }
    class VolumeMount {
        +String name
        +String mountPath
        +Boolean readOnly
    }
    class Volume {
        +String name
        +HostPath hostPath
        +Secret secret
    }
    class Secret {
        +String secretName
        +Item[] items
    }
    class Port {
        +String name
        +Int port
    }
    class Env {
        +String name
        +String value
        +ValueFrom valueFrom
    }
    DcgmExporter --> Metadata
    DcgmExporter --> Spec
    Spec --> Affinity
    Spec --> VolumeMount
    Spec --> Volume
    Spec --> Port
    Spec --> Env
    Affinity --> NodeAffinity
    Volume --> Secret
```

## Diagram 5

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Pending: Create DcgmExporter
    Pending --> Scheduling: Resource created
    Scheduling --> NodeSelection: Evaluate nodeSelector
    NodeSelection --> AffinityCheck: OS=linux
    AffinityCheck --> NodeMatched: GPU instance & not fargate
    AffinityCheck --> Scheduling: No matching node
    NodeMatched --> MountingVolumes: Node assigned
    MountingVolumes --> MountingPodResources: Mount pod-gpu-resources
    MountingPodResources --> MountingTLS: Mount dcgmtls secret
    MountingTLS --> ConfiguringEnv: Set environment variables
    ConfiguringEnv --> StartingContainer: DCGM_EXPORTER_KUBERNETES=true
    StartingContainer --> InitializingDCGM: Container running
    InitializingDCGM --> LoadingTLS: Load TLS config
    LoadingTLS --> LoadingMetrics: Configure cert/key
    LoadingMetrics --> Running: Load metrics config
    Running --> [*]: Pod deleted
```

## Diagram 6

```mermaid
graph TD
    A[Metrics Collected] --> B[DCGM_FI_DEV_GPU_UTIL]
    A --> C[DCGM_FI_DEV_MEM_COPY_UTIL]
    A --> D[DCGM_FI_DEV_FB_FREE]
    A --> E[DCGM_FI_DEV_FB_USED]
    A --> F[DCGM_FI_DEV_FB_TOTAL]
    A --> G[DCGM_FI_DEV_FB_USED_PERCENT]
    A --> H[DCGM_FI_DEV_MEMORY_TEMP]
    A --> I[DCGM_FI_DEV_GPU_TEMP]
    A --> J[DCGM_FI_DEV_POWER_USAGE]
    B --> K[GPU Utilization %]
    C --> L[Memory Utilization %]
    D --> M[FB Memory Free MiB]
    E --> N[FB Memory Used MiB]
    F --> O[FB Memory Total MiB]
    G --> P[FB Used Percentage]
    H --> Q[Memory Temperature C]
    I --> R[GPU Temperature C]
    J --> S[Power Draw W]
```
